<TD WIDTH="9%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;1.01</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement. </B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">The information described below under &#147;Item 2.03. Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant&#148; is hereby incorporated by reference into this Item 1.01.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;2.03</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant. </B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January 18, 2010, we entered into Amendment No. 1 to Acquisition and Refinancing Bridge Credit Agreement (the &#147;Amendment&#148;), among the lenders
named therein and Citibank, N.A., as paying agent, to amend our Acquisition and Refinancing Bridge Credit Agreement dated as of November 9, 2009 (as amended, the &#147;Agreement&#148;), among the lenders named therein, Deutsche Bank Securities Inc.,
Citigroup Global Markets Inc. and HSBC Securities (USA) Inc., as joint bookrunners, and Deutsche Bank AG Cayman Island Branch and Citibank, N.A., as co-administrative agents. The Agreement was amended to increase the term loan facility by &pound;1.6
billion to an aggregate of &pound;7.1 billion. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We expect to use the borrowings under the Agreement, or if available, proceeds from
alternative financing sources, to finance the proposed acquisition of Cadbury plc and to refinance certain indebtedness of Cadbury plc and its subsidiaries. Borrowings under the Agreement are also available for general corporate purposes of Kraft
Foods and our subsidiaries. Some of the lenders under the Agreement and their affiliates have various relationships with us and our subsidiaries involving the provision of financial services, including cash management, investment banking and trust
services. In addition, we and certain of our subsidiaries have entered into foreign exchange and other derivative arrangements with certain of the lenders and their affiliates. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The foregoing description of the Amendment is qualified in its entirety by reference to the complete terms and conditions of the Amendment, which is filed as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form
8-K and is incorporated by reference into this Item&nbsp;2.03. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;7.01</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Regulation FD Disclosure. </B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This
information shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act,
except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in that filing. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January&nbsp;19, 2010, Kraft Foods Inc., a Virginia
corporation, issued an announcement describing the detailed terms of a recommended final offer to acquire each outstanding ordinary share of Cadbury plc (the &#147;Offer&#148;). A copy of the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.2 and is
incorporated by reference into this Item&nbsp;7.01. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January&nbsp;19, 2010, we issued a letter to our shareholders relating to the
cancellation of our special meeting of shareholders scheduled for February&nbsp;1, 2010. On January&nbsp;19, 2010, we also distributed the Chairman and CEO&#146;s message to employees regarding the Offer. Copies of the letter to shareholders and the
Chairman and CEO&#146;s message to employees are attached hereto as Exhibits&nbsp;99.3 and 99.4. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January&nbsp;19, 2010, our independent
registered accounting firm, PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP (&#147;PwC&#148;), delivered to us a currently dated and reissued report on our profit estimate regarding earnings per share. This report was prepared at our request to meet our obligations
under The City Code on Takeovers and Mergers (the &#147;Takeover Code&#148;) issued by The Panel on Takeovers and Mergers in connection with the Offer. A copy of our profit estimate, the bases for the profit estimate and a copy of the profit
estimate report are furnished as Exhibits 99.5 and 99.6 to this report. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January&nbsp;19, 2010, Lazard&nbsp;&amp; Co., Limited, Centerview
Partners UK LLP, Citigroup Global Markets Limited and Deutsche Bank AG, London Branch (together, the &#147;Financial Advisors&#148;) delivered to us a currently dated and reissued report on our profit estimate regarding earnings per share. This
report was prepared at our request to enable us to meet our obligations under the Takeover Code in connection with the Offer. A copy of the Financial Advisors&#146; report is furnished as Exhibit 99.7 to this report. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January&nbsp;19, 2010, the Kraft Foods Board of Directors made a statement pursuant to Rule 28.5 of the Takeover Code regarding the discretionary cash
flow guidance first announced on November&nbsp;3, 2009 and PwC and the Financial Advisors each indicated that they have no objection to their respective reports in respect of that discretionary cash flow guidance (as set out in the document dated
December&nbsp;4, 2009 issued by us in connection with the Offer) continuing to apply. A copy of this statement and confirmation is furnished as Exhibit 99.8 to this report. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On January&nbsp;19, 2010, we issued a notification of publication on our website of revised offer documents in connection with the Offer. A copy of the website notification is furnished as Exhibit 99.9 to
this report. </FONT></P>

<DESCRIPTION>AMENDMENT NO.1 TO ACQUISITION AND REFINANCING BRIDGE CREDIT AGREEMENT

<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Amendment No.1 to Acquisition and Refinancing Bridge Credit Agreement</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>AMENDMENT NO. 1 TO ACQUISITION AND REFINANCING </U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><U>BRIDGE CREDIT AGREEMENT </U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">AMENDMENT NO. 1, dated as of January&nbsp;18, 2010 (this
&#147;<U>Amendment</U>&#148;), among Kraft Foods Inc., a Virginia corporation (&#147;<U>Kraft</U>&#148;), Citibank, N.A. (&#147;<U>Citi</U>&#148;), as Paying Agent (the &#147;<U>Paying Agent</U>&#148;) and the lenders set forth on the signature
pages hereto (the &#147;<U>Committing Lenders</U>&#148;) to the Acquisition and Refinancing Bridge Credit Agreement dated as of November&nbsp;9, 2009 (as amended, modified or supplemented from time to time, the &#147;<U>Credit Agreement</U>&#148;)
among Kraft, the Lenders from time to time party thereto, Citi and Deutsche Bank AG Cayman Islands Branch (&#147;<U>DB</U>&#148;), as co-administrative agents, the Paying Agent; HSBC Securities (USA) Inc., as syndication agent and DB, as
documentation agent. Capitalized terms used herein but not otherwise defined shall have the meanings assigned to such terms in the Credit Agreement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">WHEREAS, pursuant to Section&nbsp;9.01 thereof, the Credit Agreement may be amended to increase the Commitments of any consenting Lenders with the written consent of the Paying Agent, Kraft and any such
consenting Lenders; and </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">WHEREAS, each of the Committing Lenders has agreed to increase its respective Commitment under the
Credit Agreement in the manner set forth herein. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the premises and covenants contained
herein and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which are hereby acknowledged, the parties hereto, intending to be legally bound hereby, agree as follows: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;1. <U>Amendments</U>.</B> Schedule I of the Credit Agreement is hereby deleted and replaced in its entirety with Schedule I
attached hereto. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;2. <U>Representations and Warranties</U>.</B> Kraft hereby represents and warrants to the
Paying Agent and the Lenders as of the date hereof that: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) The execution, delivery and performance of this Amendment have
been duly authorized by all necessary corporate action by Kraft and do not contravene (i)&nbsp;the charter or by-laws of Kraft or (ii)&nbsp;in any material respect, any law, rule, regulation or order of any court or governmental agency or any
contractual restriction binding on or affecting Kraft; and </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) After giving effect to this Amendment, the representations and
warranties set forth in the Credit Agreement are true and correct in all material respects on and as of the date hereof, except to the extent that such representations and warranties specifically refer to an earlier date, in which case they shall be
true and correct in all material respects as of such earlier date. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;3. <U>Conditions to Effectiveness</U>.</B>
This Amendment shall become effective on the date on which each of the following conditions is satisfied or waived: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) The
Administrative Agents shall have executed this Amendment and the Administrative Agents (or their counsel) shall have received an executed counterpart of this Amendment from Kraft and each of the Committing Lenders; </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) The Administrative Agents shall have received for the account of each Lender a
certificate signed by a duly authorized officer of Kraft, dated the date hereof, stating that: (i)&nbsp;the representations and warranties contained in Section&nbsp;4.01 of the Credit Agreement are correct on and as of the date hereof, and
(ii)&nbsp;no event has occurred and is continuing on and as of the date hereof that constitutes a Default or Event of Default; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">(c) The Administrative Agents shall have received on or before the date hereof the following, each dated such day, in form and substance satisfactory to the Administrative Agents: (i)&nbsp;certified copies of the resolutions of the Board of
Directors of Kraft approving this Amendment, including the increase in Commitments hereunder, and of all documents evidencing other necessary corporate action and governmental approvals, if any, with respect to this Amendment, and (ii)&nbsp;a
certificate of the Secretary or an Assistant Secretary of Kraft certifying the names and true signatures of the officers of Kraft authorized to sign this Amendment and the other documents to be delivered hereunder; and </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d) The Administrative Agents shall have received favorable written opinions of (A)&nbsp;Cravath, Swaine&nbsp;&amp; Moore LLP, special New
York counsel to Kraft, (B)&nbsp;Hunton&nbsp;&amp; Williams LLP, special Virginia counsel to Kraft and (C)&nbsp;internal counsel for Kraft of Cravath, in each case, in form and substance reasonably satisfactory to the Administrative Agents.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Paying Agent shall notify Kraft and the Lenders of the date on which this Amendment shall have become effective upon satisfaction or
waiver of all of the conditions precedent set forth in this Section&nbsp;3. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Paying Agent and the Committing Lenders agree and acknowledge
that they may not, in relation to this Amendment and the increase in the Commitments contemplated hereby, take any action or do any thing described in paragraphs (a)&nbsp;through (e)&nbsp;of Section&nbsp;3.04 of the Credit Agreement: (i)&nbsp;in
relation to any misrepresentation or misstatement made under or in relation to this Amendment or contained in any document delivered pursuant to this Section&nbsp;3 (unless such misrepresentation or misstatement constitutes a Certain Funds Event of
Default); or (ii)&nbsp;because or as a result of any condition precedent to effectiveness of this Amendment set out in this Section&nbsp;3 subsequently being determined not to have been satisfied. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;4. <U>Fees</U>.</B> Kraft agrees to pay to each of the Committing Lenders and their affiliates all fees owing to the
Committing Lenders and their affiliates as separately agreed in writing by Kraft and the Committing Lenders or their affiliates. Kraft further agrees that the failure to pay any such fees shall constitute an Event of Default under
Section&nbsp;6.01(a) of the Credit Agreement as if such fees were payable in accordance with Section&nbsp;2.08 thereof. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">-2- </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;5. <U>Counterparts</U>.</B> This Amendment may be executed in any number of
counterparts and by different parties hereto on separate counterparts, each of which when so executed and delivered shall be deemed to be an original, but all of which when taken together shall constitute a single instrument. Delivery of an executed
counterpart of a signature page of this Amendment by facsimile transmission or email shall be effective as delivery of a manually executed counterpart hereof. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;6. <U>Applicable Law</U>.</B> THIS AMENDMENT SHALL BE GOVERNED BY, AND CONSTRUED IN ACCORDANCE WITH, THE SUBSTANTIVE LAWS OF THE STATE OF NEW YORK WITHOUT REGARD TO CHOICE OF LAW
DOCTRINES. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;7. <U>Headings</U>.</B> The headings of this Amendment are for purposes of reference only and
shall not limit or otherwise affect the meaning hereof. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:8%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Section&nbsp;8. <U>Effect of Amendment</U>.</B> Except as
expressly set forth herein, this Amendment shall not by implication or otherwise limit, impair, constitute a waiver of or otherwise affect the rights and remedies of the Lenders or the Agents under the Credit Agreement or any other documents related
thereto, and, save as expressly set forth herein, shall not alter, modify, amend or in any way affect any of the terms, conditions, obligations, covenants or agreements contained in the Credit Agreement or any other provision of the Credit Agreement
or any document related thereto, all of which are ratified and affirmed in all respects and shall continue in full force and effect. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">[SIGNATURE PAGES FOLLOW] </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.2 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">NOT FOR RELEASE, PUBLICATION OR DISTRIBUTION, IN WHOLE OR IN PART, IN, INTO OR FROM JAPAN OR ANY OTHER JURISDICTION WHERE TO DO SO WOULD CONSTITUTE A VIOLATION OF THE RELEVANT LAWS OF THAT JURISDICTION
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For Immediate Release </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">19&nbsp;January 2010 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>RECOMMENDED FINAL* OFFER </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>by </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>KRAFT FOODS INC. (&#147;KRAFT FOODS&#148;) </B>
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>for </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><B>CADBURY PLC (&#147;CADBURY&#148;) </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>VALUING EACH CADBURY SHARE AT 840 PENCE </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>SUMMARY </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Recommended Final Offer
terms </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

recommends Cadbury Securityholders to accept the terms of the Final Offer. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under the terms of the Final Offer, Cadbury Securityholders will be entitled to receive: </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">representing, in aggregate, 840 pence per Cadbury Share and GBP 33.60&nbsp;per Cadbury ADS.

Kraft Foods and Cadbury. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>An attractive valuation and substantial long-term value creation potential as part of the
Combined Group </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Management and employees </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The combination will augment the world-class capabilities of both Kraft Foods and Cadbury by employing a &#147;best of both&#148; approach, from sales
and marketing to distribution and management. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In particular, Kraft Foods believes that the global business network of the Combined Group will create opportunities for Cadbury employees and

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In addition, Kraft Foods has given assurances to Cadbury that, on the Final Offer becoming or being declared wholly unconditional, the existing

of the Final Offer </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods also announces that it reserves the right to, and intends to, reduce the number of acceptances required to fulfil the Acceptance Condition
from 90&nbsp;per cent. to 50&nbsp;per cent. plus one Cadbury Share on or after 26&nbsp;January 2010. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Final Offer does not require the approval of Kraft Foods Shareholders. Accordingly, the condition relating to such approval, as set out in the
Original Offer Documents, is treated as satisfied for the purposes of the Final Offer. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Full acceptance of the Final Offer will result in the issue of 265&nbsp;million New Kraft Foods Shares, representing approximately 18&nbsp;per cent. of
the existing issued share capital and 15&nbsp;per cent. of the enlarged issued share capital of Kraft Foods. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Commenting on
the Offer, Irene Rosenfeld, Chairman and CEO of Kraft Foods, said: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We have great respect for Cadbury&#146;s brands, heritage and
people. We believe they will thrive as part of Kraft Foods. This recommended offer represents a compelling opportunity for Cadbury Shareholders, providing both immediate value certainty and upside potential in the combined company. For Kraft Foods
Shareholders it transforms the portfolio, accelerates long-term growth and delivers highly attractive returns, while maintaining financial discipline.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">3 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Commenting on the Offer, Roger Carr, Chairman of Cadbury, said: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We believe the offer represents good value for Cadbury shareholders and are pleased with the commitment that Kraft Foods has made to our heritage,
values and people throughout the world. We will now work with the Kraft Foods&#146; management to ensure the continued success and growth of the business for the benefit of our customers, consumers and employees.&#148; </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Cadbury Securityholders who have previously accepted the Original Offer (and have not withdrawn those acceptances) will automatically be deemed to have
accepted the terms of the Final Offer by virtue of their prior acceptances and therefore need take no further action. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Other Cadbury
Securityholders who wish to accept the recommended Final Offer must take action to accept the Final Offer by 1.00 pm (London time) / 8.00 am (New York City time) on 2&nbsp;February 2010.</B> Details of the procedure for doing so will be set out in
the Final Offer Documents (and, in the case of certificated Cadbury Shares and Cadbury ADSs, the Final Acceptance Forms) to be sent to Cadbury Securityholders as soon as practicable. The Final Offer Documents will also be available on Kraft
Foods&#146; website (www.transactioninfo.com/kraftfoods/).<B> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This summary should be read in conjunction with the full text of the
following announcement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">* The Offer is final and will not be increased, except that Kraft Foods reserves the right to increase the Offer if

STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">19&nbsp;January 2010 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>RECOMMENDED FINAL<FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(1)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"> OFFER </FONT></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>by </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>KRAFT FOODS INC. (&#147;KRAFT FOODS&#148;) </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>for </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>CADBURY PLC (&#147;CADBURY&#148;) </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>VALUING EACH CADBURY SHARE AT 840 PENCE </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Introduction </B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The
board of Kraft Foods is pleased to announce the detailed terms of a recommended Final</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(1)</SUP></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> Offer to acquire the entire issued and to be issued share capital of Cadbury. The board of Cadbury unanimously recommends Cadbury Securityholders to accept the terms of the Final Offer. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>The Final<FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(1)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> Offer </FONT></B></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under the terms of the Final Offer, Cadbury Securityholders will be entitled to receive: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

SIZE="2"><B>and</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>0.1874 New Kraft Foods Shares</B></FONT></P></TD></TR>

SIZE="2"><B>and</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>0.7496 New Kraft Foods Shares</B></FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">representing, in aggregate, 840 pence per Cadbury Share and GBP 33.60&nbsp;per Cadbury ADS (based on
the closing share price of USD 29.58&nbsp;per Kraft Foods Share on 15&nbsp;January 2010, the last trading day prior to the date of this announcement, and an exchange rate of USD 1.63 to GBP 1.00 as at 18&nbsp;January 2010). </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">8 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In addition, Cadbury has advised Kraft Foods that Cadbury Shareholders will be receiving
10 pence per Cadbury Share by way of a Special Dividend. This will, in effect, enable Cadbury Shareholders to receive 10 pence out of the planned final dividend of 12.3 pence per share previously announced by Cadbury, subject to board and
shareholder approval, which would otherwise not become payable.</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(2)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Assuming the vesting and exercise of all share options and awards under the Cadbury Share Schemes: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">the Final Offer values the entire issued and to be issued share capital of Cadbury at approximately GBP 11.9 billion; and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">265&nbsp;million New Kraft Foods Shares will be issued (assuming full acceptance of the Final Offer), representing approximately 18&nbsp;per cent. of
the existing share capital and 15&nbsp;per cent. of the enlarged share capital of Kraft Foods. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The terms of the Final Offer
supersede those of the Original Offer. The terms of the Original Offer are no longer capable of acceptance. Further information in relation to the Final Offer is set out in sections 11 and 16 of this announcement. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Mix and Match Facility </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Cadbury
Securityholders who accept the Final Offer may make elections under the Mix and Match Facility. Under the Mix and Match Facility, accepting Cadbury Securityholders may elect to vary the proportions in which they receive New Kraft Foods Shares and
cash consideration, subject to off-setting elections being made by other Cadbury Securityholders. To the extent that elections cannot be satisfied in full, they will be scaled down on a pro-rata basis. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Reduction of Acceptance Condition </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">Kraft Foods also announces that it reserves the right to, and intends to, reduce the number of acceptances required to fulfil the Acceptance Condition from 90&nbsp;per cent. to 50&nbsp;per cent. plus one Cadbury Share on or after
26&nbsp;January 2010. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If the Acceptance Condition is satisfied and all other Conditions have been satisfied, fulfilled or, to the extent
permitted, waived, the Offer will be declared wholly unconditional at that time and withdrawal rights will terminate (except in limited circumstances). Cadbury Securityholders who have already accepted the Offer, but whose willingness to accept the
Offer is affected by the reduction of the Acceptance Condition, may wish to consider withdrawing their acceptances with respect to such Cadbury Shares promptly. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">9 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Condition regarding approval of Kraft Foods Shareholders </I></B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The issue of New Kraft Foods Shares pursuant to the Final Offer does not require the approval of Kraft Foods Shareholders. Accordingly, the condition
relating to such approvals is treated as satisfied for the purposes of the Final Offer. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>3.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>The creation of a global leader in the food and confectionery industry</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The board of Kraft Foods believes that a combination of Kraft Foods and Cadbury represents a strong and complementary strategic fit, creating a global confectionery leader, with a portfolio including more
than 40 confectionery brands, each with annual sales in excess of USD 100 million. Globally, the Combined Group would be number one in the chocolate and sugar confectionery segments and a strong number two in the high growth gum segment.
Cadbury&#146;s leading brands, such as <I>Cadbury</I>, <I>Trident</I> and <I>Halls</I>, are highly complementary to Kraft Foods&#146; portfolio and would benefit from Kraft Foods&#146; global scope, scale and array of proprietary technologies and
processes. In addition, the acquisition of Cadbury will significantly enhance the strength of Kraft Foods&#146; presence in the confectionery sector, enabling Kraft Foods to leverage Cadbury&#146;s product development capabilities. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods believes that confectionery markets are consolidating and scale is becoming increasingly important, in part due to retailers&#146; increasing
bargaining power, control of the supply chain and growing portfolio of their own retailer brands, which have benefited from the global economic climate. The combination of Kraft Foods and Cadbury provides the Combined Group with important additional
scale to compete even more effectively in the confectionery sector. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods and Cadbury have highly complementary geographic footprints.
Importantly, a combination would increase scale for both companies in developing markets such as Brazil, Russia and China, where Kraft Foods has a stronger presence, and India, Mexico and South Africa, where Cadbury holds leading positions. The
Combined Group would also benefit from an improved position across Europe, including in France and Spain. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">10 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods&#146; and Cadbury&#146;s routes to market are also highly complementary. Kraft Foods is
particularly strong in the grocery channel in North America and Western Europe, while Cadbury is well positioned in instant consumption channels, which have become increasingly important in both developed and developing markets. A combination
provides an enhanced platform for the Combined Group to distribute both Cadbury&#146;s and Kraft Foods&#146; products through both channels, creating an attractive opportunity for higher growth and margins. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>4.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>The Final Offer represents an attractive opportunity for Cadbury Securityholders</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Final Offer equates to an enterprise value multiple of 13.0 times Cadbury&#146;s underlying 2009 EBITDA</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(3)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">, based on the closing share price of USD 29.58&nbsp;per Kraft Foods
Share on 15&nbsp;January 2010, and an exchange rate of USD 1.63 to GBP 1.00 as at 18&nbsp;January 2010. The enterprise value multiple is calculated assuming the exercise of all share options and vesting of all share awards held under the Cadbury
Share Schemes. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>5.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Substantial synergy benefits</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">The combination of Kraft Foods and Cadbury is expected to provide the potential for meaningful revenue synergies over time from investments in distribution, marketing and product development. In addition, it is expected that pre-tax cost
savings of at least USD 675&nbsp;million annually can be realised by the end of the third year following completion. Total one-off implementation cash costs of approximately USD 1.3 billion are expected to be incurred in the first three years
following completion.</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(4)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Both Kraft Foods and Cadbury have implemented extensive cost saving and operating efficiency programmes in recent years and have already delivered
significant margin improvement and revenue growth improvements. These annual cost savings are still expected to be achieved over and above the current performance improvement plans at each of Kraft Foods and Cadbury (including Cadbury&#146;s updated
Vision into Action programme). While it is anticipated that these targeted savings will continue to be delivered, Kraft Foods believes that the Combined Group would be capable of achieving substantial further cost savings through economies of scale
and procurement benefits, general and administrative cost savings and marketing and selling costs savings. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">11 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Cadbury Securityholders are able to share in the synergies resulting from the combination of Kraft Foods and
Cadbury through the share component of the Offer. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>6.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Recommendation</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>The board of Cadbury,
which has been so advised by Goldman Sachs International, Morgan Stanley&nbsp;&amp; Co. Limited and UBS Investment Bank considers the terms of the Final Offer to be fair and reasonable. In providing their financial advice to the board of Cadbury,
Goldman Sachs International, Morgan Stanley&nbsp;&amp; Co. Limited and UBS Investment Bank have taken into account the board&#146;s commercial assessments. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Accordingly, the board of Cadbury unanimously recommends Cadbury Securityholders to accept the terms of the Final Offer. </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

SIZE="2">Kraft Foods believes that the Final Offer will deliver the following key benefits: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">accretion to earnings per share in 2011 of approximately USD 0.05 on a cash basis; and</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(4)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">a mid teens return on investment, well in excess of Kraft Foods&#146; cost of capital</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP

7&nbsp;September 2009: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">accretion to earnings in the second year following completion on a cash basis</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP

non-cash items such as the amortisation of intangibles after acquisition); </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">retention of Kraft Foods&#146; investment-grade credit rating; and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">maintenance of Kraft Foods&#146; dividend. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">12 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Following the combination with Cadbury, Kraft Foods expects to revise its long-term
growth targets to 5+&nbsp;per cent. for revenue and 9-11&nbsp;per cent. for earnings per share, from its previously announced 4+&nbsp;per cent. and 7-9&nbsp;per cent. respectively.</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(4)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In
addition, the acquisition is expected to enhance the quality of the Combined Group&#146;s earnings, and create a business with strong discretionary cash flow generation and attractive revenue growth prospects across a diversified portfolio of brands
and product groups worldwide. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>8.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Financing the cash consideration</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft
Foods is providing the cash consideration payable by it under the Final Offer from its own resources, funds available from an amended bridge facility that has been arranged by a syndicate of banks and/or proceeds from alternative financing sources.
A summary of the amended bridge facility will be included in the Final Offer Documents. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Lazard&nbsp;&amp; Co., Limited, Centerview Partners
UK LLP, Citigroup Global Markets Limited and Deutsche Bank AG, London Branch are satisfied that sufficient resources are available to Kraft Foods to satisfy in full the cash consideration payable by it as a result of full acceptance of the Final
Offer. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>9.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Management, employees and locations</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods believes that the combination of Cadbury and Kraft Foods represents a strong, complementary fit and expects that the combination will enhance the Combined Group&#146;s growth
profile</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(3)</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">. The combination will augment the world-class
capabilities of both Kraft Foods and Cadbury by employing a &#147;best of both&#148; approach, from sales and marketing to distribution and management. In particular, Kraft Foods believes that the global business network of the Combined Group will
create opportunities for Cadbury employees and managers. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In addition, Kraft Foods has given assurances to Cadbury that, on the Offer becoming
or being declared wholly unconditional, the existing contractual employment rights, including pension rights, of all Cadbury Group employees will be fully safeguarded. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;
</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">13 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>10.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Kraft Foods offers an excellent investment opportunity</B> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Kraft Foods believes that scale is important in the global food industry </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As the
world&#146;s second largest food company, with 2008 revenues of USD 41.9 billion, Kraft Foods has significant global scale, with operations in more than 70 countries. While the US is a key market and Kraft Foods is the number one food company there
based on retail sales, Kraft Foods generated approximately half of its revenues from outside the US in 2008 and sells its products in approximately 150 countries around the world. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods believes that its portfolio of leading brands is one of the strongest in the global food industry, with nine of its brands generating annual revenues exceeding USD 1 billion each. Kraft
Foods&#146; objective is to be the category leader in its principal markets and it generates 80&nbsp;per cent. of its revenues from categories in which it holds the number one position. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Over the past three years, Kraft Foods&#146; management has successfully re-positioned the company for sustainable, profitable growth by reframing its categories, capitalising on its established sales
capabilities and driving down costs without compromising its commitment to high quality. Kraft Foods&#146; strategy is centred on marketing and developing leading consumer brands and pursuing growth opportunities to deliver shareholder value. Kraft
Foods remains confident in meeting its long-term performance targets. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Kraft Foods has upgraded its EPS guidance </I></B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:3px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On 12&nbsp;January 2010, Kraft Foods increased its guidance for 2009 diluted earnings per share, to at least USD 2.00 (up approximately
five per cent. from 2008) versus the previous expectation of at least USD 1.97</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(5)</SUP></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">. This increased guidance reflects strong operating gains as well as a significant increase in marketing investments versus the prior year. Kraft Foods expects to achieve this level of diluted earnings
per share while continuing to increase investment behind its brands, with advertising and consumer marketing spending expected to grow to approximately 7&nbsp;per cent. of sales in 2009 from 6.7&nbsp;per cent. of sales in 2008. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>Kraft Foods&#146; share price </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Since
the announcement of its possible offer for Cadbury on 7&nbsp;September 2009, Kraft Foods believes its share price performance has been adversely affected by a number of factors of a short-term nature, including: (i)&nbsp;concern that it will not
maintain financial discipline regarding an acquisition of Cadbury; (ii)&nbsp;concern that the issuance of Kraft Foods Shares to certain Cadbury Securityholders may result in &#147;flowback&#148; of such shares; and (iii)&nbsp;short selling activity.
Kraft Foods believes that, following completion of its acquisition of Cadbury, these short-term pressures on its share price should dissipate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">14 </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">By way of illustration, Kraft Foods notes the following: </FONT></P> <P

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods has historically traded on a current year price earnings multiple broadly in line with that of the S&amp;P 500 Index. Based on Kraft
Foods&#146; own guidance for its 2009 diluted earnings per share of at least USD 2.00</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">(5)</SUP></FONT><FONT

Cadbury ADSs, the Final Acceptance Forms) to be sent to Cadbury Securityholders as soon as practicable. The Final Offer Documents will also be available on Kraft Foods&#146; website (www.transactioninfo.com/kraftfoods/).<B> </B></FONT></P> <P

continuing to provide: (a)&nbsp;accepting Cadbury Securityholders with the Mix and Match Facility, which Kraft Foods has determined will remain open until the end of the Subsequent Offer Period; (b)&nbsp;a facility under which accepting Cadbury
Shareholders may elect to receive all cash consideration to which they are entitled in US dollars, if they do not wish to receive it in pounds sterling; (c)&nbsp;a facility under which accepting Cadbury ADS Holders may elect to receive all cash
consideration to which they are entitled in pounds sterling, if they do not wish to receive it in US dollars; (d)&nbsp;a facility under which accepting Cadbury Shareholders will, subject to certain exceptions, receive New Kraft Foods Shares in the
form of CDIs, which are capable of being held, transferred and settled in CREST; and (e)&nbsp;a designated UK agent to assist small shareholders resident in certain jurisdictions in holding, trading and managing their CDI interests in the New Kraft
Foods Shares. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Further details of the Mix and Match Facility, currency elections and Kraft Foods CDIs are set out in the Original Offer

(www.transactioninfo.com/kraftfoods/) and, together with the Final Acceptance Forms, on request from the Receiving Agent or the US Information Agent (as applicable). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<DESCRIPTION>LETTER TO KRAFT FOODS SHAREHOLDERS
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Letter to Kraft Foods Shareholders</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.3 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center">

<IMG SRC="g40537g15e75.jpg" ALT="LOGO"> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">January&nbsp;19, 2010 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Dear Fellow Shareholder: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We are pleased to provide you with an update on our
proposed acquisition of Cadbury plc. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Today, we made a final offer that the Board of Directors of Cadbury plc has unanimously
recommended that its shareholders accept. Our final offer consists of 500 pence in cash and 0.1874 shares of Kraft Foods common stock for each outstanding Cadbury ordinary share, including each Cadbury ordinary share represented by a Cadbury
American Depositary Share. We reached this excellent result by maintaining a highly disciplined approach, staying well within our stated financial criteria and focusing on the compelling rationale for combining Kraft Foods and Cadbury. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">From a financial perspective, we expect the transaction to deliver excellent returns to our shareholders. We believe it will: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">be approximately $0.05 accretive to earnings per share in 2011 on a cash basis (which excludes the one-time expenses related to the acquisition and the
impact of non-cash items such as the amortization of intangibles from the acquisition); </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">yield a mid-teens internal rate of return; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">enable us to maintain our investment-grade rating; and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">enable us to maintain our dividend per share. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Further, we expect to increase our long-term revenue growth target to 5+% and our long-term EPS growth target to 9-11%. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">From a strategic perspective, we believe the combination of Kraft Foods and Cadbury will: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">create a strong combined portfolio with leading market positions in the fast-growing confectionery category; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">have a significantly strengthened footprint in developing markets, with enhanced scale; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">benefit from world-class infrastructure in traditional and instant consumption channels; and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">offer meaningful revenue synergies and significant cost savings. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Put simply, we believe that Kraft Foods and Cadbury are a perfect strategic fit. With Cadbury&#146;s support and cooperation, we can move
quickly and efficiently to realize the full benefits that we expect from this transaction. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Your Board is pleased that we have
fulfilled the desire expressed by many of you to minimize our use of Kraft Foods stock in the transaction. The final offer greatly reduces the number of Kraft Foods shares we will issue to acquire Cadbury to an estimated 265&nbsp;million shares from
as many as 370&nbsp;million shares in our prior offer. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The aggregate share component of the final offer is below the 20%
threshold set by the New York Stock Exchange rules for shareholder approval. As a result, we do not have a basis under UK regulations to condition the final offer we announced today on a shareholder vote. Accordingly, the Special Meeting that we had
scheduled for February&nbsp;1, 2010 is canceled. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On behalf of your Board, I thank you for your continued support. I am pleased that we are
pursuing this transformational acquisition in a way that we believe will deliver significant long-term value for Kraft Foods and all of our shareholders. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This letter contains forward-looking statements
regarding Kraft Foods&#146; offer to combine with Cadbury. Such statements include, but are not limited to, statements about the benefits of the proposed combination and other such statements that are not historical facts, which are or may be based
on Kraft Foods&#146; plans, estimates and projections. These forward-looking statements are subject to a number of risks and uncertainties, many of which are beyond Kraft Foods&#146; control, that could cause Kraft Foods&#146; actual results to
differ materially from those indicated in any such forward-looking statements. Such factors include, but are not limited to, failure to obtain necessary regulatory approvals or required financing or to satisfy any of the other conditions to the
offer, and the risk factors, as they may be amended from time to time, set forth in Kraft Foods&#146; filings with the US Securities and Exchange Commission (&#147;SEC&#148;), including the registration statement on Form S-4, as amended from time to
time, filed by Kraft Foods in connection with the offer, Kraft Foods&#146; most recently filed Annual Report on Form 10-K and subsequent reports on Forms 10-Q and 8-K. Kraft Foods disclaims and does not undertake any obligation to update or revise
any forward-looking statement in this letter, except as required by applicable law or regulation. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Additional US-Related Information </B>

<DESCRIPTION>KRAFT FOODS PROFIT ESTIMATE REPORT
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Kraft Foods Profit Estimate Report</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.5 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>PROFIT ESTIMATE FOR THE KRAFT FOODS GROUP FOR THE YEAR ENDING 31 DECEMBER 2009 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>1.
GENERAL </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Kraft Foods made the following public statement on 12 January 2010 within a public announcement: <I>&#147;Kraft Foods increased
its guidance for 2009 diluted earnings per share to at least US$2.00 versus the previous expectation of at least US$1.97&#148;</I>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Diluted
earnings per share is defined as net earnings attributable to Kraft Foods divided by weighted average diluted shares. Weighted average shares for diluted earnings per share adds back incremental shares from assumed conversions of stock options, net
of assumed share repurchases and LTIP shares to the weighted average shares of basic earnings per share. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The statement regarding diluted
earnings per share for the year ended 31 December 2009 constitutes a profit estimate for the purposes of the Takeover Code (the<B> &#147;Profit Estimate&#148;</B>). The Kraft Foods Directors have considered and reconfirm the Profit Estimate.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Profit Estimate includes an estimate for certain costs in connection with Kraft Foods&#146; possible combination with Cadbury that are
recognisable under US GAAP. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Profit Estimate comprises diluted earnings per share rather than statutory earnings from continuing
operations before income taxes, as diluted earnings per share is one of the primary profit measures historically used by Kraft Foods in its external reporting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>2. BASIS OF PREPARATION </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Profit Estimate has been prepared on a basis consistent with
the accounting policies of Kraft Foods, which are in accordance with US GAAP and those which Kraft Foods anticipates will be applicable for the full year ended 31 December 2009. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Kraft Foods Directors have prepared the Profit Estimate based on the unaudited interim condensed consolidated financial statements for the nine months ended 30 September 2009, the unaudited management
accounts for the two months ended 30 November 2009 and an estimate of the results for Kraft Foods for the one month period ended 31 December 2009. </FONT></P>

those shown in the Profit Estimate and the difference may be material. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our work on the Profit Estimate does not constitute an audit. Our work
has not been carried out in accordance with auditing or other standards and practices generally accepted in the United States of America, or other jurisdictions (other than in the United Kingdom), nor the auditing standards and practices of the
Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (United States), nor does it constitute an examination, compilation or review under those standards and practices. Accordingly, it should not be relied upon as if it had been carried out in accordance with
those standards and practices. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Opinion </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In our opinion, the Profit Estimate has been properly compiled on the basis stated and the basis of accounting used is consistent with the accounting policies of the Kraft Foods Group. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Yours faithfully </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">/s/ PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>DEALING DISCLOSURE REQUIREMENTS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under the provisions of Rule 8.3 of the U.K. Takeover Code (the &#147;<B>Code</B>&#148;), if any person is or becomes &#147;interested&#148; (directly or indirectly) in 1&nbsp;per cent. or more of any
class of &#147;relevant securities&#148; of Kraft Foods or of Cadbury plc, all &#147;dealings&#148; in any &#147;relevant securities&#148; of that company (including by means of an option in respect of, or a derivative referenced to, any such
&#147;relevant securities&#148;) must be publicly disclosed by no later than 10:30 a.m. (New York City time) / 3:30 p.m. (London time) on the London business day following the date of the relevant transaction. This requirement will continue until
the date on which the Offer becomes, or is declared, unconditional as to acceptances, lapses or is otherwise withdrawn or on which the &#147;offer period&#148; otherwise ends. If two or more persons act together pursuant to an agreement or
understanding, whether formal or informal, to acquire an &#147;interest&#148; in &#147;relevant securities&#148; of Kraft Foods or of Cadbury plc, they will be deemed to be a single person for the purpose of Rule 8.3. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Under the provisions of Rule 8.1 of the Code, all &#147;dealings&#148; in &#147;&#145;relevant securities&#148; of Kraft Foods or Cadbury plc by Kraft Foods
or Cadbury plc, or by any of their respective &#147;associates&#148;, must be disclosed by no later than 7:00 a.m. (New York City time) / 12:00 noon (London time) on the London business day following the date of the relevant transaction. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A disclosure table, giving details of the companies in whose &#147;relevant securities&#148; &#147;dealings&#148; should be disclosed, and the number of
such securities in issue, can be found on the website of the U.K. Panel on Takeovers and Mergers (the &#147;<B>U.K. Takeover Panel</B>&#148;) at <I><U>www.thetakeoverpanel.org.uk</U></I>. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Interests in securities&#148; arise, in summary, when a person has long economic exposure, whether conditional or absolute, to changes in the price of
&#147;relevant securities&#148;. In particular, a person will be treated as having an &#147;interest&#148; by virtue of the ownership or control of securities, or by virtue of any option in respect of, or derivative referenced to, securities.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Terms in quotation marks are defined in the Code, which can also be found on the U.K. Takeover Panel&#146;s website. If you are in any doubt
as to whether or not you are required to disclose a &#147;dealing&#148; under Rule 8, you should consult the U.K. Takeover Panel. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"
